commit e51719e6b1fabf18530f0f7a0a7e9bf5eecb8edd
Author: Martin Jansa <martin.jansa@lge.com>
Date:   20210908

    Jenkins: Fix unityci based docker image
    
    * switches from ubuntu-18.04 to ubuntu-20.04 to fix vulkan renderer
    
    * install libvulkan1 and remove ca-certificates
    * update the comments
    
    * we're using -force-vulkan in our builds
    
    * install libvulkan1 as it was before the switch to unityci docker image
      because without this Unity will fail to detect Vulkan and use llvmpipe
      renderer instead, which results in all black preview images in Assets
      bundles and we also use -force-vulkan, so it's a bit surprising that
      missing libvulkan1 wasn't fatal error
    
    * without mesa-vulkan-drivers vulkaninfo would fail with:
      root@0ea8660cc34a:/# vulkaninfo
      ERROR: [Loader Message] Code 0 : loader_scanned_icd_add: Could not get 'vkCreateInstance' via 'vk_icdGetInstanceProcAddr' for ICD libGLX_nvidia.so.0
      Cannot create Vulkan instance.
      This problem is often caused by a faulty installation of the Vulkan driver or attempting to use a GPU that does not support Vulkan.
      /build/vulkan-tools-KEbD_A/vulkan-tools-1.2.131.1+dfsg1/vulkaninfo/vulkaninfo.h:371: failed with ERROR_INCOMPATIBLE_DRIVER
    
      but having mesa-vulkan-drivers in the image breaks Unity trying to use Vulkan
    
    * I don't see ca-certificates being used
    
    * use latest hdrp/unityci/editor docker image built in:
      https://auto-jenkins.lgsvl.net/view/docker/job/unityci-docker-image/28/
    
    * don't use xvfb-run
    
    * update image-info-lgsvl.source
      when starting from editor-lgsvl instead of regular editor from Docker Hub
      the /opt/unity/image-info-lgsvl.source would already be there
      but we don't overwrite it, instead add another section after
      IMAGE_APP="unity-editor-simulator"
      showing few more details, but drop UNITY_CHANGESET, UNITY_MODULES
      params as they are never set when building ${UNITY_DOCKER_IMAGE_TAG}-simulator
      image and we "inherit" them from editor-lgsvl image used in EDITOR_DOCKER_IMAGE

commit 95caf278b293744e69800bad9687fd32141c6880
Author: Eugene Agafonov <eugene.agafonov@lge.com>
Date:   20210819

    AUTO-6872: Adopt docker terminology
    
    Docker Registry VS Repository VS Image VS Tag
    
    https://developers.redhat.com/blog/2016/01/13/a-practical-introduction-to-docker-container-terminology#repository
    
    TL;DR:
    1. Image is Repository + Tag
    2. Same string could be either a repository or an image implying
    `latest` tag
    
    Example:
    
    Docker Hub's `amazon/aws-cli:latest` is an image where `amazon/aws-cli`
    is the Repository and `latest` is the Tag
    
    ```
    minikube:30080/svlcontent/testcaserunner/pythonapi:v42
    <- registry ->|
    <---------- repository -------------------------->|tag
    ```
    
    The Registry is a hosting service for Repositories.
    Docker Hub is just a registry that is used by default.

      https://auto-gitlab.lgsvl.net/HDRP/Simulator/commit/08038b7a2b87e1608aebe757e74d6acd774006fb#b8a2054485aa4aa693a454077a9753bb5fed45cc
      but it doesn't exist in master causing:
      04:10:58  Assets/Scripts/ScenarioEditor/Managers/ScenarioManager.cs(310,13): error CS0103: The name 'IsInitializing' does not exist in the current context
    
    * and assign to private isInitialized property directly to fix:
      04:10:58  Assets/Scripts/ScenarioEditor/Managers/ScenarioManager.cs(311,13): error CS0200: Property or indexer 'ScenarioManager.IsInitialized' cannot be assigned to -- it is read only

    AUTO-6545: Docker/README.md, Docker/run.sh: Update for 2021.1 release
    
    - The LINK TO CLOUD button does not function when Simulator is run
      inside of a container, so instruct users to first run it outside of
      the containser. Modify the mapping of the container's
      /root/.config/unity3d so that this works.
    
    - Add a note that only the "API Only" and "Random Traffic" runtime
      templates can be used and that the "OPEN BROWSER" and "Visual Editor"

commit 5d3a47dec90886706e9d8d69159aba304673e93c
Author: Martin Jansa <martin.jansa@lge.com>
Date:   20210219

    [Build] Jenkins: Show better error message when SCENARIOS_RUNNER_DOCKER_TAG is missing or empty
    
    * https://auto-jenkins.lgsvl.net/job/simulator-release-cloud/30 failed with:
    
      [Pipeline] { (bundleScenariosRunner)
      [Pipeline] dir
      03:57:22  Running in /home/jenkins/workspace/simulator-cloud-release-2019.3.15f1/Jenkins
      [Pipeline] {
      [Pipeline] sh
      03:57:23  + docker pull auto-gitlab.lgsvl.net:4567/
      03:57:23  invalid reference format
      03:57:23  + echo ABORT: cannot pull auto-gitlab.lgsvl.net:4567/
      03:57:23  ABORT: cannot pull auto-gitlab.lgsvl.net:4567/
      03:57:23  + exit 1
    
    * because newly added parameter isn't added in jenkins job until the updated pipeline
      is executed at least once and unfortunately, when it's not picked there yet,
      it won't even use the default value specified in the pipeline and will just
      run with empty value which might cause unexpected build failures like this
    
    * use ${env.OUTPUT_SUFFIX} instead of ${OUTPUT_SUFFIX}, because when "error"
      triggers "post" early it fails with:
      groovy.lang.MissingPropertyException: No such property: OUTPUT_SUFFIX for class: groovy.lang.Binding
      as in:
      https://auto-jenkins.lgsvl.net/view/Jenkins%20test/job/simulator-jansa-jenkins-wip-test/123/console
    
    * testing params.SCENARIOS_RUNNER_DOCKER_TAG for null isn't enough,
      because it isn't null as long as the parameter definition appears
      in parameters section
    
    * testing all params for empty doesn't help much as well, because some like
      BUILD_SIMULATOR_* in Bundle jobs could be intentinally set to empty
    
    * unfortunatelly jenkins pipeline documentation still lacks:
      https://issues.jenkins.io/browse/INFRA-1053

commit f8ae5f5f178707838475d73fc4bc358389206d08
Author: Martin Jansa <martin.jansa@lge.com>
Date:   20210218

    [AUTO-6141] Jenkins: rename the scenarios runner docker image before save and set matching default in the scenario_runner.sh
    
    * otherwise it will try to load:
      TestCaseRunner/scenarioRunner/docker/auto-gitlab.lgsvl.net-4567-hdrp-scenarios-runner-dev.tar
      because that's the default in the script and fail, because the docker image is actually
      ${GITLAB_HOST}:4567/\$SCENARIOS_RUNNER_DOCKER_TAG
      where SCENARIOS_RUNNER_DOCKER_TAG is the jenkins job parameter
    
    * use more unique tag for it:
      simulator-build__${OUTPUT_SUFFIX}
      because with the default SCENARIOS_RUNNER_DOCKER_TAG value:
      hdrp/scenarios/runner/jenkins:latest
      it would happily reuse older "latest" local image even if the bundled
      tarball was already updated, by including the build number or
      git tag for releases we ensure that the right image is loaded
    
    [AUTO-6141] Scenario Runner: Incorrect tarball name

        Branch name is used to generate filenames, but filename shall not
        contain any slashes

commit 4423c13387868a1ec7590bcebc737e3ff36a8eb3
Author: Eugene Agafonov <eugene.agafonov@lge.com>
Date:   20200403

    AUTO-3044: Fix possible race condition while getting git commit hash
    
    `git rev-parse HEAD` in environment section is performed by Jenkins
    server. If new commit appers on the branch after the job is scheduled,
    Jenkins agent would checkout newer commit while GIT_COMMIT refers to the
    old one.
    
    To fix the race condition lets call `git rev-parse HEAD` on Jenkins
    agent after the code is checked out.

    NPCController now adds distributed components to wheels transforms.
    Checking if the distributed component exists before adding new from the script (if the component is included in the prefab).
    Renamed "camera" field to "sensorCamera" in a few sensors to remove build warning.

commit f0a7aa84220343f791d8d7ecf56fba3a728986e6
Author: Karol Byczkowski <karol.byczkowski@lge.com>
Date:   20191209

    Added support for the cluster simulation.
    
    [6d7c96d] Disabled sensors do not unregister from agent controller.
    
    [fb408cd] Added SensorsController which manages all the sensors attached to an agent.
    The sensors setup moved from AgentManager to SensorsController.
    SensorBase uses new property "CanBeDelegatedToClient" to determine if the sensor should be instantiated only in the master simulation or in a client simulation.
    Sensors that can be distributed to a client simulation: ColorCameraSensor, DepthCameraSensor, GroundTruth2DSensor, GroundTruth2DSensorVisualizer, GroundTruth3DSensor, GroundTruth3DSensorVisualizer, LidarSensor, RadarSensor, SemanticCameraSensor.
    
    [391f8c6] NPCController distributes the lights' states from master to clients.
    Lowered the update time of LiteNetLib managers from 15ms to 5ms.
    Increased the extrapolation limit in MockedRigidbody from 0.1s to 0.3s.
    Added RemoteTimeTicksDifference to IPeerManager.
    TimeManager uses ticks instead of total milliseconds.
    Added remote time ticks difference when poping time difference to convert remote timestamp to local timestamp.
    Encapsulated clients list to public property in the MasterManager.
    Loader now starts network master before starting the simulator manager.
    
    [cb6eaf6] States of the agent vehicle's lights are distributed to the clients.
    Fixed PedestrianController setting the incorrect speed to the distributedAnimator when it stops.
    
    [6ddd68c] NPCManager distributes vehicle color from master to clients.
    TimeManager uses the difference between epoch time and UTC now in total milliseconds.
    ByteCompression supports color.
    Fixed PedestrainController - using Animator if DistributedAnimator is unavailable.
    
    [5a315ed] MockedRigidbody extrapolates velocities no longer than 100ms after receiving last snapshot.
    
    [f9e5c6c] Improved extrapolation of the velocities in mocked rigidbody.
    MessagesManager no longer dispatches received messages on the main thread as pool events are called in an Update method.
    TimeManager now synchronizes the time with the authoritative master, timestamps indicate UTC of sending the message, synchronization can be delayed and timestamps before synchronization may be invalid.
    Added TimeDifference to message (time difference between sending message and TimeManager start).
    CompressFloatToInt method in ByteCompression now uses bytes count instead of a max int value.
    Added PushCompressedVector3 and PopDecompressedVector3 to ByteCompression.
    BytesStack now supports double.
    
    [4a63883] Network API update.
    All unicast, broadcast and receive messages methods now use Message class as a parameter.
    Message object contains address key (string), content (BytesStack), type (MessageType), timestamp (DateTime).
    Added TimeManager which handles the message timestamp based on time difference to initial network message.
    Added DistributedControllable, which extends MonoBehaviour and implements IControllable, it broadcast all control actions from master to clients.
    BytesStack now supports long integers.
    
    [1f9b938] Improved distributing the elements of the Simulation.
    Optimized DistributedAnimator, sending only changed float if required instead of a whole snapshot.
    Mocked rigidbody of the agent extrapolates position and rotation based on a recent and previous snapshot.
    NPCManager and PedestrianManager send initial position and rotation when spawning entity.
    MapSignal distributes the ControlCommands from master to clients.
    All awaiting messages (from the previous simulation) are cleared when the client connects to the master again.
    Removed MockingSimulationType ExtrapolateFromVelocity.
    BytesStack now properly push and pop empty string.
    
    [9773958] Master and client properly stop the simulations when the master receives a stop request from WebUI.
    Distributing pedestrians from master to the clients.
    Added DistributedAnimator and MockedAnimator synchronizing the parameters (triggers are not yet supported).
    DistributedObject sends enable and disable commands to corresponding MockedObject.
    Renamed methods in the ByteCompression - "write" to "push" and "read" to "pop, methods using BytesStack became BytesStack extension methods.
    Added PushEnum and PopEnum extension to BytesStack in the ByteCompression class.
    BytesStack now supports float and bool values, methods for integers use 4 bytes as default.
    
    [b00a4bd] (WIP) Added distribution of the agent and NPCs.
    SimulationNetwork data added as a SimulatorManager property.
    RequiredBytes<T> added to the ByteCompression, which returns the count of required bytes for encoding enum to int.
    
    [c453f4e] Added core of the dedicated server-client architecture to the Simulator.
